<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накал.html>нака́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nakál</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накал.html>нака́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накал.html>нака́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накал.html>нака́лов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>incandescence
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:белый.html>бе́лый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:накал.html>нака́л</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bélyj nakál</i> ― <span class="e-translation">white heat</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:красный.html>кра́сный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:накал.html>нака́л</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">krásnyj nakál</i> ― <span class="e-translation">red heat</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>tension, heat
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накал.html>нака́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:борьба.html>борьбы́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nakál borʹbý</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the heat of the struggle</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:накалить.html>накалённый</a> (19559)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накалить.html>накалённый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nakaljónnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past passive perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накалить.html>накали́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nakalítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накалить.html>накалённый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nakaljónnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>incandescent, red-hot</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> tense, strained
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:накалённый.html>накалённая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:обстановка.html>обстано́вка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nakaljónnaja</b> obstanóvka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">tense situation</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> red-hot, furious, ready to flare up</li></ol>

***накалить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:накалить.html>накали́ть</a> (19559)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">кали́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kalítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накалить.html>накали́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nakalítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">нака́ливать</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">накаля́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to heat to a very high temperature (metal or something metallic)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:накалить.html>накали́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:докрасна.html>докрасна́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nakalítʹ</b> dokrasna</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make red-hot</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:накалить.html>накали́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:добела.html>добела́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nakalítʹ</b> dobelá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make white-hot</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to agitate, to stir up, to build up tension in</li></ol>

***накалиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:накалиться.html>накали́ться</a> (26838)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накалить.html>накали́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nakalítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накалиться.html>накали́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nakalítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накаляться.html>накаля́ться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">нака́ливаться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to heat up to a high temperature, to become very hot</li>
<li>to become extremely tense
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обстановка.html>обстано́вка</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:накалиться.html>накали́лась</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">obstanóvka <b>nakalílasʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the situation escalated</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">the situation <b>became extremely tense</b></span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накалить.html>накали́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nakalítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">накаля́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nakaljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накаляться.html>накаля́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nakaljátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накалиться.html>накали́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to heat up to a high temperature, to become very hot</li>
<li>to become extremely tense

<p>Univerbation of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:канун.html>кану́не</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kanúne</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накануне.html>накану́не</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nakanúne</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>the day before</li>
<li>on the eve of
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:накануне.html>накану́не</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вечер.html>ве́чером</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nakanúne</b> véčerom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">overnight</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***накапливаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:накапливаться.html>нака́пливаться</a> (12116)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накапливать.html>нака́пливать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nakáplivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накапливаться.html>нака́пливаться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nakáplivatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накопиться.html>накопи́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to accumulate, to gather, to amass</li>

<li><a href = vnd.unilang:механизм.html>механи́зм</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> накатывания, наматывания <a href = vnd.unilang:бумага.html>бума́ги</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> бумагоделательной <a href = vnd.unilang:машина.html>маши́не</a> <span style="display: none"></span></span> <span class="example-fullblock example-absent-block"><ul>

***накатать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:накатать.html>наката́ть</a> (18573)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катать.html>ката́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">katátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накатать.html>наката́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nakatátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накатывать.html>нака́тывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to make smooth <i>(by rolling)</i></li>
<li>to roll on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:накатать.html>наката́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:краска.html>кра́ску</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nakatátʹ</b> krásku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to roll the paint on</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to roll up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:накатать.html>наката́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:шарик.html>ша́риков</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хлеб.html>хлеба</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nakatátʹ</b> šárikov iz xleba</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to roll up a few bread balls</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dash off, to throw together, to fling off, to fling together, to tear off
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:накатать.html>наката́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:письмо.html>письмо́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nakatátʹ</b> pisʹmó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to dash off a letter</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***накатить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:накатить.html>накати́ть</a> (18390)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катить.html>кати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">katítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накатить.html>накати́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nakatítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накатывать.html>нака́тывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to roll <i>(on, onto)</i></li>
<li><i>(waves)</i> to roll in, to coast in</li>
<li><i>(weather)</i> to set in, <i>(events)</i> to begin, to break out</li>
<li><i>(feelings, mood)</i> to come <i>(over)</i>, to be seized <i>(with)</i>, to have an attack</li>
<li><i>(alcohol)</i> to drink strong liquor, to especially vodka</li>
<li><i>(computer)</i> to apply patches, including installation of updates and applying cracks</li></ol>

***накатывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:накатывать.html>нака́тывать</a> (21523)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накатать.html>наката́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nakatátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накатить.html>накати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nakatítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накатывать.html>нака́тывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nakátyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накатать.html>наката́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накатить.html>накати́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to make smooth <i>(by rolling)</i>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накатать.html>наката́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nakatátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to roll on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накатать.html>наката́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:краска.html>кра́ску</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nakatátʹ krásku</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to roll the paint on</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накатать.html>наката́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nakatátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to roll <i>(on, onto)</i>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накатить.html>накати́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nakatítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(waves)</i> to roll in, to coast in
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накатить.html>накати́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nakatítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(weather)</i> to set in, <i>(events)</i> to begin, to break out
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накатить.html>накати́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nakatítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(feelings, mood)</i> to come <i>(over)</i>, to be seized <i>(with)</i>, to have an attack
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накатить.html>накати́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nakatítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:накачать.html>накача́ть</a> (17600)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:качать.html>кача́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kačátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накачать.html>накача́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nakačátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накачивать.html>нака́чивать</a></b>)
</p>

<li>to inflate</li></ol>

***накидывавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:накидывать.html>наки́дывавший</a> (24930)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накидывать.html>наки́дывавший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nakídyvavšij</span>)

***накидывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:накидывать.html>наки́дывать</a> (24930)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">наки́д-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nakíd-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накидывать.html>наки́дывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nakídyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накинуть.html>наки́нуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to throw on, to throw over
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:накидывать.html>наки́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nakídyvatʹ</b> na sebjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to slip on; slip over one's shoulders</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to add
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:накидывать.html>наки́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:цена.html>це́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nakídyvatʹ</b> cénu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to mark up the price</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">наки́дываться</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nakídyvatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накинуться.html>наки́нуться</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nakínutʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***накинуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:накинуть.html>наки́нуть</a> (5525)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кинуть.html>ки́нуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kínutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накинуть.html>наки́нуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nakínutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накидывать.html>наки́дывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to throw on, to throw over
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:накинуть.html>наки́нуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nakínutʹ</b> na sebjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to slip on; slip over one's shoulders</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to add
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:накинуть.html>наки́нь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:десяток.html>деся́тку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nakínʹ</b> desjátku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">add ten</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:накинуться.html>наки́нуться</a> (14392)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накинуть.html>наки́нуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nakínutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накинуться.html>наки́нуться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nakínutʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">наки́дываться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fall <i>(upon, on)</i>, to pounce <i>(on)</i>, to attack, to assault, to go <i>(for)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собака.html>соба́ка</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:накинуться.html>наки́нулась</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sobáka <b>nakínulasʹ</b> na menjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the dog went for [pounced on/at] me</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to fall <i>(upon, on)</i>, to pounce <i>(on)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:накинуться.html>наки́нуться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>еду</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nakínutʹsja</b> na jedu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fall on the food</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:накинуться.html>наки́нуться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nakínutʹsja</b> na knígu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pounce on a book; snatch at a book</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:накинуться.html>наки́нуться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:предложение.html>предложе́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nakínutʹsja</b> na predložénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pounce on the offer</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to come down <i>(on)</i>, to jump <i>(on)</i>, to jump all over</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накинуть.html>наки́нуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nakínutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наброситься.html>набро́ситься</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nabrósitʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:накладка.html>накла́дка</a> (19574)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">накла́д(ывать)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">naklád(yvatʹ)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накладка.html>накла́дка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nakládka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накладка.html>накла́дки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накладка.html>накла́дки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накладка.html>накла́док</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>(of a lock)</i> cover plate, cover strap, cover piece</li>
<li>hairpiece, false hair</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> slip, blunder, mess-up, error
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́тим</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выйти.html>вы́шла</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:накладка.html>накла́дка</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s étim výšla <b>nakládka</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">there was a problem/mess-up with that</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
